<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1981–82 UEFA Cup</h1>

<p>The <b>1981–82 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a></b> was won by <a href="/wiki/IFK_G%C3%B6teborg" title="IFK Göteborg">IFK Göteborg</a> on aggregate over <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Association_team_allocation">Association team allocation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Association team allocation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A total of 64 teams from 32 <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> member associations participate in the 1981–82 UEFA Cup. The association ranking based on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_country_coefficient" title="UEFA country coefficient">UEFA country coefficients</a> is used to determine the number of participating teams for each association:</p>
<ul>
<li>Associations 1, 2 and 5 each have four teams qualify.</li>
<li>Associations 3–4 and 7-9 each have three teams qualify.</li>
<li>Associations 9–22 (except Wales) each have two teams qualify.</li>
<li>Associations 23–33 each have one team qualify.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Association_ranking">Association ranking</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Association ranking">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>For the 1981–82 UEFA Cup, the associations are allocated places according to their 1981 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_country_coefficient" title="UEFA country coefficient">UEFA country coefficients</a>, which takes into account their performance in European competitions from 1976–77 to 1980–81.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Teams">Teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The labels in the parentheses show how each team qualified for competition:</p>
<ul>
<li>TH: Title holders</li>
<li>CW: Cup winners</li>
<li>CR: Cup runners-up</li>
<li>LC: League Cup winners</li>
<li>2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, etc.: League position</li>
<li>P-W: End-of-season European competition play-offs winners</li>
</ul>

<tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_leg_2">First leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: First leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_3">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_leg_5">First leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: First leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_5">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1981%E2%80%9382_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
